if PostgreSQL is connected)\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    if (config.env === \'development\' && postgresConnected) {\n      try {\n require(\'rate-limit-redis\');\n  redis = require(\'../config/redis\');\n  // Check if redis is a mock client\n  if (redis && typeof redis.ping === \'function\') {\n    useRedis = true;\n  }\n} catch (error) {\n  console.warn(\'  rate-limit-redis not available, using memory store\');\n  useRedis = false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Create rate limiter configuration\n */\nfunction createLimiterConfig(options) {\n  const baseConfig = {\n    windowMs: options.windowMs,\n    max: options.max,\n    standardHeaders: true,\n    legacyHeaders: false,\n    handler: (req, res) => {\n      return errorResponse(\n        res,\n        429,\n        options.message || \'Too many requests, please try again later\'\n      );\n    },\n    skip: options.skip || (() => false),\n  };\n\n  // Add Redis store if      console.warn(\'  Could not create Redis store, using memory store\');\n    }\n  }\n\n  return baseConfig;\n}\n\n/**\n * General API rate limiter\n */\nconst apiLimiter = rateLimit(createLimiterConfig({\n  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes\n  max: 5, // 5 requests per window\n  prefix: \'rl:auth:\',\n  message: \'Too many authentication attempts, please try again after 15 minutes\',\n}));\n\n/**\n * Rate limiter for file uploads\n */\nconst uploadLimiter = rateLimit(createLimiterConfig({\n  windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hour\n  max: 20, // 20 uploads per hour\n  prefix: \'rl:upload:\',\n  message: \'Upload limit exceeded, please try again later\',\n}));\n\n/**\n * Rate limiter for password reset\n */\nconst passwordResetLimiter = after 1 hour\',\n}));\n\n/**\n * Rate limiter for email verification\n */\nconst emailVerificationLimiter = rateLimit(createLimiterConfig({\n  windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hour\n  max: 3, // 3 requests per hour\n  prefix: \'rl:email:\',\n  message: \'Too many verification emails sent, please try again after 1 hour\',\n}));\n\nmodule.exports = {\n  apiLimiter,\n  authLimiter,\n
